<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выселить.html>вы́селить</a> (15822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сели́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">selítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выселить.html>вы́селить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výselitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выселять.html>выселя́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выселять.html>выселя́ть</a> (25668)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выселить.html>вы́селить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výselitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выселять.html>выселя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyseljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выселить.html>вы́селить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to evict, to expel</li>
<li>to evacuate, to resettle</li></ol>

***высечь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высечь.html>вы́сечь</a> (12615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высечь.html>вы́сечь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsečʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высекать.html>высека́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hew, to carve, to sculpt, to cut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высечь.html>вы́сечь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надпись.html>на́дпись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надгробный.html>надгро́бном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мне</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výsečʹ</b> nádpisʹ na nadgróbnom kámne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>carve</b> the inscription on the gravestone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скульптор.html>ску́льптор</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:высечь.html>вы́сек</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мрамор.html>мра́мора</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:статуя.html>ста́тую</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Skúlʹptor <b>výsek</b> iz mrámora státuju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The sculptor <b>carved</b> the statue from marble.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высечь.html>вы́сечь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výsečʹ</b> ogónʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike fire (from a flint)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to whip <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">as a punishment</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толпа.html>толпа́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наброситься.html>набро́силась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>ни́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гиканье.html>ги́каньем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ругань.html>ру́ганью</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:раздел.html>разде́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:почти.html>почти́</a> донага́ <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жестокий.html>жесто́ко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:высечь.html>вы́секла</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tolpá nabrósilasʹ na níx s gíkanʹjem i rúganʹju, razdéla ix počtí donagá i žestóko <b>výsekla</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The crowd attacked them with a whooping and swearing, undressed them nearly naked and <b>flogged</b> them severely.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сечь.html>сечь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***выситься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выситься.html>вы́ситься</a> (9521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высь.html>высь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vysʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выситься.html>вы́ситься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возвыситься.html>возвы́ситься</a></b>)

***выскакивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выскакивать.html>выска́кивать</a> (6271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́скок-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výskok-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выскакивать.html>выска́кивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyskákivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выскочить.html>вы́скочить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to jump out, to leap out</li>
<li>to appear, to come up (of a sore, pimple, etc.)</li>
<li>to drop out, to fall out</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выскользнуть.html>вы́скользнуть</a> (9061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skolʹznútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выскользнуть.html>вы́скользнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výskolʹznutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выскальзывать.html>выска́льзывать</a></b>)
</p>

***выскочить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выскочить.html>вы́скочить</a> (1555)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vy-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-скочи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skočítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">q.v.</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выскочить.html>вы́скочить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výskočitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выскакивать.html>выска́кивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to jump out, to leap out</li>
<li>to appear, to come up (of a sore, pimple, etc.)</li>
<li>to drop out, to fall out</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выслать.html>вы́слать</a> (5114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>слать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выслать.html>вы́слать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výslatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высылать.html>высыла́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to send, to dispatch, to send forward</li>
<li>to banish, to exile; to deport, to expel</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выследить.html>вы́следить</a> (14798)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следить.html>следи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sledítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выследить.html>вы́следить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsleditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выслеживать.html>высле́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to trail, to follow</li>
<li>to track down</li></ol>
